[30;1m4 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m5 | [0m[35mParsimonious aims to be the fastest arbitrary-lookahead parser written in pure[0m
[30;1m6 | [0m[35mPythonâ€”and the most usable. It's based on parsing expression grammars (PEGs),[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35mwhich means you feed it a simplified sort of EBNF notation. Parsimonious was[0m
[30;1m8 | [0m[35mdesigned to undergird a MediaWiki parser that wouldn't take 5 seconds or a GB[0m
[30;1m9 | [0m[35mof RAM to do one page, but it's applicable to all sorts of languages.[0m
[30;1m10 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m189 | [0m[35m==========================[0m
[30;1m190 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m191 | [0m[35mPEG parsers don't draw a distinction between lexing and parsing; everything is[0m
[30;1m192 | [0m[35mdone at once. As a result, there is no lookahead limit, as there is with, for[0m
[30;1m193 | [0m[35minstance, Yacc. And, due to both of these properties, PEG grammars are easier[0m
[30;1m194 | [0m[35mto write: they're basically just a more practical dialect of EBNF. With[0m
[30;1m195 | [0m[35mcaching, they take O(grammar size * text length) memory (though I plan to do[0m

[30;1m31 | [0m[35mParsimonious aims to be the fastest arbitrary-lookahead parser written in pure[0m
[30;1m32 | [0m[35mPythonâ€”and the most usable. It's based on parsing expression grammars (PEGs),[0m
[30;1m33 | [0m[35mwhich means you feed it a simplified sort of EBNF notation. Parsimonious was[0m
[30;1m34 | [0m[35mdesigned to undergird a MediaWiki parser that wouldn't take 5 seconds or a GB[0m
[30;1m35 | [0m[35mof RAM to do one page, but it's applicable to all sorts of languages.[0m
[30;1m36 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m216 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m217 | [0m[35mPEG parsers don't draw a distinction between lexing and parsing; everything is[0m
[30;1m218 | [0m[35mdone at once. As a result, there is no lookahead limit, as there is with, for[0m
[30;1m219 | [0m[35minstance, Yacc. And, due to both of these properties, PEG grammars are easier[0m
[30;1m220 | [0m[35mto write: they're basically just a more practical dialect of EBNF. With[0m
[30;1m221 | [0m[35mcaching, they take O(grammar size * text length) memory (though I plan to do[0m

[30;1m219 | [0m[35minstance, Yacc. And, due to both of these properties, PEG grammars are easier[0m
[30;1m220 | [0m[35mto write: they're basically just a more practical dialect of EBNF. With[0m
[30;1m221 | [0m[35mcaching, they take O(grammar size * text length) memory (though I plan to do[0m
